Eleven out of sixteen, also supported by two others in several or at least some areas, particularly given its multi-ethnic composition, constitutes a significant majority in any democracy. It were these reports, Madam, that resulted in the JVP which was a party to the APRC walking out of the exercise. A dialogue unfortunately does not find a place in the political programme of the JVP except in their own terms. I must state, Madam, that President Mahinda Rajapaksa certainly had no control over the actions of the JVP. The country knows about the MoU signed between the Government and the main Opposition Party, the UNP, the objective of which was to evolve a consensus on the national question. Such a consensus would have ensured a two-thirds majority in Parliament for the type of solution that the President outlined in the course of his inaugural address to the APRC and the Experts Panel and such an agreement between the Government and the main Opposition Party would have also ensured the required approval for any solution at a referendum in the country. Very unfortunately, the President by accommodating deserters from the UNP, for whatever reason, was prepared to sacrifice the Memorandum of Understanding signed with the UNP with all its attendant advantages and this, I think, was a singularly unfortunate event but history was repeating itself. I do not wish to go into the intricacies of this piece of political skulduggery but the President in my view could have saved the situation if he was prepared to stand tall above all others, if in fact he was truly focussed on a solution and looking at the issue from the point of view of the larger and long term interests of the country because the destiny of the country

[ගරු ආර්. සම්පන්දන් මහතා]

2008 ෙපබරවාරි 06 719 720

was at this time in his hands. Unfortunately that was not to be and the official UNP consequently dropped out of the APRC process. Meanwhile, the Chairman of the APRC, a Gentleman for whom I have the highest regard, was continuing with his efforts. He came up with his own report and the parties continued with their discussions at the APRC. It was at this point of time that the President's party, the Sri Lanka Freedom Party came up with its proposals, "A Unitary System of Government with the District as the Unit of Devolution". The basic features of the proposals outlined by the Sri Lanka Freedom Party before the APRC was indeed a far cry from what the President stated in his inaugural address to the APRC. He talked of maximum autonomy, genuine autonomy in keeping with models of governance in other parts of the world including India with people being able to determine their own destiny in the territories where they lived. So this was a far cry from what the President said in his inaugural address to the APRC and the Experts Panel, and I must state quite frankly the two positions that were outlined by the SLFP and by the President in the course of his inaugural address were irreconcilable. I might say with due respect, the President had plunged from the sublime to the ridiculous. There was no way in which the President could redeem himself thereafter. I must state that it was after this position of the SLFP before the APRC, that I for the first time commented on the APRC process and said that that process was as dead as a door nail. I was certain that after such proposals from the SLFP, the APRC could never take off. The Chairman and some of the parties continued to be at work. The process was delayed. The Budget became the cause of further delay. The JVP having walked out of the APRC wanted to wreck the APRC and it was extracting its pound of flesh. Small nationalist parties within the APRC encouraged by the SLFP proposals were meeting the President and complaining against some features that the Chairman of the APRC and some of the other parties were endeavoring to incorporate in the proposals. These meetings were taking place quietly on one side while the APRC was sitting - without the participation of all APRC Members - between some of the ultra-nationalist parties and the President. The international community had for long been insisting upon a credible set of devolution proposals that were sustainable. On Saturday the 12th of January, the Co-Chairs issued a statement in regard to this matter. I would like to read from that statement. It states, I quote: “The Co - Chairs support a continued Norwegian role as facilitator. The Co-Chairs emphasize their belief that there is no military solution to the conflict in Sri Lanka, and reiterate their support for a negotiated settlement. Thus they urge the government of Sri Lanka to finalize a politically sustainable devolution plan; urge all parties to comply with their obligations under international law to protect civilians and allow access by humanitarian aid agencies to populations in need; express deep concern about the human rights situation and protection of civilians in

Sri Lanka, and call for continued monitoring of the human rights situation by such means as to assure an appropriate role for the U.N. and request the government of Sri Lanka to provide access to the Liberation Tigers of Tamil Eelam in Kilinochchi for representatives of the Co-Chairs and the facilitator.”

That was a comprehensive statement which dealt with the need for a set of political proposals outlining a sustainable devolution programme and also makes a special emphasis on the human rights situation on the question of humanitarian access to civilians who were victims of the conflict and in regard to access for the Co-Chairs and the facilitator to the LTTE in Kilinochchi.

This was the situation in which the President had to now deal with the nationalist parties maintaining a constant contact with him and with the SLFP having placed these proposals before the APRC. The President could not displease the nationalist parties. He fixed 23rd January as the date for the final report. He also had to make sure that the final report did not displease the nationalist parties. He had to fix a date to satisfy the international community that something has been done and it was in these circumstances that a stratagem had to be devised to extricate himself from the quandary he had landed himself in. He had all along endeavoured to impress upon the international community that he was genuinely committed to an acceptable political solution. The international community was insisting on results. He was not able to deliver because the nationalist parties would not permit him to go beyond his own party's proposals before the APRC and they were not prepared to accommodate or accept the proposals being made by the APRC Chairman and the other parties of the APRC. The only way that the President could devise was to ask the APRC to take its own time to finalize their own proposals and seek refuge in the outdated Thirteenth Amendment to the Constitution which was already a part of the Constitution of Sri Lanka from 1987. It was 20 years old and the person who, at the inaugural meeting of the APRC wanted them to come up with something new, something in keeping with the pattern of devolution that prevailed in other countries the world over that would give the people the right to determine their own destiny in the territories where they lived; the person who talked about maximum devolution and the person who said, “I will not impose a solution on the country, I leave it to you; you and the Panel of Experts can decide and submit your report”, was compelled to seek refuge in something 20 years old, which had been in the Constitution for over two decades.

By this time the Ceasefire Agreement too had been abrogated by the Government and therefore, it was obligatory for the Government to do something or at least show that it was doing something and it was in these circumstances that the President sought refuge in the Thirteenth Amendment to the Constitution. Eighteen months of deliberations of the APRC with over 60

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 721 722

sittings and the Experts Panel Reports were not required for President Mahinda Rajapaksa to implement the Thirteenth Amendment to the Constitution which had been enacted in November, 1987. The Co-Chairs and the international community surely did not make their best efforts to achieve what already existed in the Constitution as a solution to the protracted conflict. For good measure, certain clauses in regard to the implementation of language provisions which had remained moribund for over two decades were also included. This was the pathetic state in which the President found himself and he had to somehow device some stratagem, some escape route. He had to seek refuge somewhere and he was able to do that when he sought refuge in the Thirteenth Amendment to the Constitution. The President had made his position very clear, Madam, in the Independence Day speech which he delivered on the 4th of February. I listened to him and I quote from the “Daily News” of 5th February, 2008 which gives its English translation, where he states: “Our solution must be based on what could be implemented in this country. We cannot offer solutions that are experiments. We cannot experiment with solutions when so much blood has been shed and tens of thousands of lives have been lost. That is why we selected a solution which can be implemented and about which we have experience. This practical solution is to bring the provincial administration closer to the people within the framework of our Constitution.” The President put the matter completely beyond doubt with this statement he made at the Independence Day celebrations which was a complete reversal of what the President said at the inaugural meeting of the APRC. He had completely reneged from the position taken up when he appointed the APRC and the Panel of Experts and that must be said, Madam, in a manner that admits of no doubt. I would like to examine what President Mahinda Rajapaksa said in his 2007 Independence Day speech and I quote from his speech which appeared in “The Hindu” of February 5, 2007. It states: “The Sinhala people were ready for a political solution on the ethnic conflict. I wish to re-emphasize that I know that the Sinhala people in the South are ready for this. We are not ready to give into the bloodthirsty demands of the LTTE. However, at the minimum we should be reasonable and honest enough to agree with Mr. Anandasangaree or the Hon. Douglas Devananda.” That is what the President said. He extended an invitation to us also on this Independence day to join with him but we are prepared to join people only when we can repose our faith and trust in them and when we are quite certain that they will keep their words. So, he on this occasion said that you must at least repose your faith in Anandasangaree and Douglas Devananda and you must

be able to satisfy them. What does Mr. Anandasangaree say in regard to a political solution? Mr. Anandasangaree addressed the final meeting of the APRC summoned in January and this is what Mr. Anandasangaree said. Though he is not a member of the APRC, he had been specially invited by the President and this is what he said. I quote: “ It is no secret that that we had been agitating for a solution based on the Federal concept….” Federal concept ! “ ….and also offered to accept the Indian Model as an alternative if the term federal is allergic to anyone. We have not changed our views in this matter and in the matter of merger of the North and the East. ” That is that the merger of the North and the East must continue. That is Anandasangaree’s position. He further goes on to say, Madam. I quote: “We assure everybody that while spurning violence we will by non-violent means and in a friendly way continue to persuade the citizens of our country to agree that no permanent solution can be found under a Unitary System.” This is what Anandasangaree says. What does Douglas Devananda say? I will quote, Madam, from an interview given by Mr. Douglas Devananda to “The Sunday Times” of 2nd of December 2007. He was asked: “ Q. Are you for the de-merger of the North and the East? A. The two provinces should be linked. We are for a united Sri Lanka within which the North-East should operate as one unit. That is our party’s view.” So, where does the President stand? Not merely had he gone back on what he said at the inaugural address when he addressed the APRC and the panel of experts, he had gone back completely on what his own Tamil supporters Anandasangaree and Douglas Devananda had been advocating and he is not able to even accommodate the views of these people. I also want to say this. While wanting to implement the Thirteenth Amendment, there is also a clear statement being made that the land powers and the police powers contained in the Thirteenth Amendment will not be given. The cause of the conflict has been that there has been grave injustice in certain areas and of those areas land and security have been vital. Those powers will not be given by a President who talked about maximum autonomy when he set up the APRC and he wanted the APRC to study other models in other parts of the world. I want to say a few words about the Thirteenth Amendment to the Constitution, Madam. I want to make it very clear that the Thirteenth Amendment to the Constitution contemplates the North-East merger. It recognizes the North-East merger which had been a reality for 18 years and which had been acted upon by successive governments and successive Presidents

[ගරු ආර්. සම්පන්දන් මහතා]

2008 ෙපබරවාරි 06 723 724

including the governments in which Mahinda Rajapaksa was both a Minister and Prime Minister. If the Thirteenth Amendment is to be implemented it can only be implemented in a merged North-East not in a separate North or in a separate East. That would be, in my submission, totally illegal; it will be immoral and it will be a fraud which nobody will accept. I want to make our position very clear in regard to that matter. I want to also say, Madam, that the Thirteenth Amendment did not drop from the sky. It emerged as a result of very lengthy discussions that took place between the J.R. Jayewardene Government in July and August, 1986 and the TULF. The Government was represented by President J. R. Jayewardene, Mr. Gamini Dissanayake, Mr. Lalith Athulath Mudali, Mr. Ronnie de Mel, Mr. A. C. S. Hameed, Mr. K. W. Devanayagam, Mr. Ranil Wickremasinghe and on the TULF side, there were Mr. Amirthalingam, Mr. Sivasithamparam, Dr. Neelan Tiruchelvam, Mr. Yogeswaran, Mr. Anandasangaree off and on and myself. I was there regularly at every sitting. We had several discussions over several days, from 9 o’ clock in the morning to 6 o’ clock in the evening, for about 10 to 15 days in July and 10 to 15 days in August, 1986. That is how the Thirteenth Amendment emerged. Based on those discussions, President Jayewardene evolved something but, that was not acceptable to us. The moment he submitted this to the Cabinet, we went and met President Jayewardene on the 29th of September, 1987. A delegation comprising of Mr. Sivasithamparam, Dr. Neelan Tiruchelvam, Mr. Yogeswaran and myself called on President Jayewardene and we told him that the draft which he had submitted to Cabinet was unacceptable, unworkable and we said that the Thirteenth Amendment must not be passed on those lines and we wrote to Prime Minister Rajiv Gandhi on the 28th of October, 1987. The letter was signed by Mr. Amirthalingam, the Secretary General of the TULF, Mr. Sivasithamparam, President of the TULF and by myself, R. Sampanthan, Vice-President of the TULF and former Member of Parliament for Trincomalee. All three of us signed this letter. It was sent to Prime Minister Rajiv Gandhi on the 28th of October, 1987. I table* the letter and want that to be included in Hansard. This is what we said in that letter, Madam. I quote:

“We feel it our duty to also express our disappointment with the proposals to solve the Tamil problem contained in the two Bills - the 13th Amendment to the Constitution and the Provincial Councils Bill - presented to Parliament by the Sri Lankan Government. These proposals do not meet the aspirations of the Tamil people nor are in any way, commensurate with the loss of life, sufferings and privations suffered by the Tamil people. Since 1983, the T.U.L.F. has always negotiated with the Government of Sri Lanka directly, utilising the good offices of the Government of India, and through the Government of India in the hope of evolving a comprehensive scheme of devolution which the T.U.L.F could commend to the Tamil people.

The T.U.L.F. regrets it cannot recommend the contents of these Bills to the Tamil people as being satisfactory, just and durable. On the eve of your departure to Sri Lanka to sign the Agreement, we requested you among other things, that a team of experts from India along with their counterparts from Sri Lanka draft the necessary legislation. You agreed that this was a reasonable request. Now the legislation is sought to be foisted on us without any Indian expert playing a part in the drafting. The T.U.L.F. expected all along that a copy of the draft legislation would be made available to the Government of India at some reasonable time before it was made public. Apprehending that this might not happen, a delegation of the T.U.L.F. met President Jayewardene on the 29th of September 1987 and made this formal request. We regret that the Bills were gazetted without being made available to the Government of India. This is not merely cavalier treatment of India but a clear breach of para 2.15 of the Agreement which states inter-alia that 'residual matters shall be resolved between India and Sri Lanka'. The Bills are certainly not the result of any such resolution.” This was contained in the letter we sent to the Prime Minister Rajiv Gandhi on 28th October, 1987. The Bills were passed in that way but at the same time, I want to say that consequent to our representations to the Government of India, President Jayewardene who had gone to Kathmandu for a SAARC Conference in November, 1987 was requested to come over to Delhi on his return from the Kathmandu SAARC Conference. Mr. Amirthalingam, Mr. Sivasithamparam and myself, the three of us were requested by the Indian Government to be present in Delhi at that time, where extensive discussions took place between the Government of India, the officials and President Jayewardene and his team and between the President and the Prime Minister of India. There were 13 matters on which President Jayewardene agreed to make improvements to the Thirteenth Amendment to the Constitution. I was present in Delhi when those discussions took place. We were in touch with the Indian officials and we know exactly what happened. But those 13 amendments were never brought about. That is the truth, Madam. In fact, on the morning that we left for New Delhi, I and my Colleagues Mr. Amirthalingam and Mr. Sivasithamparam met with Mr. Natwar Singh who was the then State Minister of Foreign Affairs in the Union Government of New Delhi and Shri Kuldip Sahadev who was the Joint Secretary to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and we were told, we - meaning the Government of India - have a firm commitment from the President to make the improvements to the Thirteenth Amendment. Mr. Kuldip Sahadev butted in and said, “We have the commitment in writing.” That is the reality. We did not contest the elections under the Provincial Councils. We refused to contest because we said that the Thirteenth Amendment is not workable and will never be a success. That is the position, Madam, with regard to the Thirteenth Amendment. Please forget it. Please dump it. We will not touch it with the wrong end of a barge pole. I want to make the Tamil position very clear on the Floor of this House. You might get hold of some quislings, some mercenaries, whom you are now

* කථාව අවසානෙය් පළ කර ඇත. உைரயினிᾠதியில் தரப்பட்ᾌள்ளᾐ. Produced at end of speech.

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 725 726

cultivating in the Eastern Province to contest elections on your behalf. But do not think you can fool the Tamil people. The Tamil people since 1956 have historically delivered certain verdicts at every election where they have stood for genuine autonomy, genuine self rule in the areas of our historical habitation, in keeping with what the President said in the course of his inaugural address to the APRC and the Panel of Experts - මූලාසනාරූඪ මන්තීතුමිය (தைலைமதாங்கும் உᾠப்பினர் அவர்கள்) (The Presiding Member) ගරු මන්තීතුමනි, ඔබතුමාට ෙවන් කර ඇති කාලය අවසානයි. ගරු ආර්. සම්පන්දන් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ஆர். சம்பந்தன்) (The Hon. R. Sampanthan)

Madam, I can go on till 12.10 p.m. and I have requested the Chief Opposition Whip to give me five more minutes. I will finish soon. I will not take your time.

In regard to the international community, Mr. P. Chidambaram, the Minister of Finance for India, and Mr. Richard Boucher, the Under-Secretary of the United States for South Asia when they were here recently and the Co-chairs have talked about the type of political solution, of radical changes in the structure of Government, genuine autonomy, which would give the people, the Tamils and the Muslims the right of self rule in the areas in which they have historically lived. I have quoted those statements in Parliament. They are in Hansard. Your Thirteenth Amendment is not anywhere close to what the international community has contemplated. Therefore, please do not try to fool anybody; please, do not try to fool yourselves. You will not be in a position to work the Thirteenth Amendment. Forget it and come clean. Think of something which people can accept.

Before I conclude, Madam, I think I must read certain answers given by the Chairman of the APRC, the Hon. (Prof.) Tissa Vitharana, in an interview he has given to "The Nation" newspaper of Sunday, 3rd February. It states, I quote:

"Q: Your credibility is at stake after the President forced you to implement something that was never discussed at the APRC under your chairmanship. What is your comment?

A: I would have preferred very much if this question of the 13th Amendment implementation had not come up till we finalized our main report. But considering the fact that this was an unforeseen development, and the fact that the Executive President of the country, the person who set up both the APC and the APRC, requested that the APRC immediately addressed what he felt was a pressing need, I as the chairman, together with the rest of the APRC, had little option but to accede to his request.”

So, it was an imposition by the President, in the words of the APRC Chairman. They merely acceded to the request of the President.

He goes on to say, I quote: “If the whole exercise was something which I was doing as a Member of my party the LSSP, or together with a few other like minded political parties, then I could have acted differently. But under the circumstances I hope the people of Sri Lanka as well as those abroad who are interested in the future of our country will understand the circumstances which have led me to follow the course that the APRC has now taken.”

There is another question, Madam, which was asked from him and which he answered. I think, I should read it very quickly. It states, I quote:

"Q: How do you interpret President Rajapaksa’s suggestion to delay the whole process?”

He wanted the process delayed. "A: The President had laid a certain deadline in January for handing over to him the final set of proposals that the APRC had been developing over the last one and a half years. But later he indicated to us that the 13th Amendment was sufficient for him to act in the interest of winning over the Tamil-speaking people,…”

That is, his quislings in Batticaloa, nobody else. “….and also to convince the international community of his commitment to a political solution to the people, and therefore we could take our time over the main set of proposals which he would be ready to receive.

Q: It is also learnt that the President had requested you to keep out land and police powers …”, which he confirms in the course of his answer.

So, what are you doing? Whom are you fooling? If you think you are fooling the Tamil people, you are sadly mistaken. Our people will never be fooled. If you think you are fooling the international community, you are sadly mistaken. The international community has clearly laid out the contours of a political settlement - what can be the solution to the problem. You are fooling yourselves. That is the most pathetic part.

Before I conclude, Madam, I would like to read a very short comment made by Mr. Rajmohan Gandhi, a very distinguished journalist and author, and a statesperson in India, the grandson of Mahatma Gandhi and also the grandson of C. Rajagopalachari, who was the first Chief Minister of Madras Presidency and also the first Governor-General of India. He is the grandson of two very distinguished people. He was asked in the course of a recent interview which he gave and which has appeared in "The Sunday Leader" of 3rd February. It states, I quote:

"Q: What lessons do you think Sri Lanka can learn from the asymmetrical devolution model now in place in India?"

The answer he gave was this. It is a long answer; I will not read the whole answer, but I will read the relevant paragraph.

He said, I quote: “If autonomy is genuine it will work. But if an offer of autonomy is mainly a façade …”

[ගරු ආර්. සම්පන්දන් මහතා]

2008 ෙපබරවාරි 06 727 728

That is what you are trying with the Thirteenth Amendment - a facade, a deceptive exercise and unworthy of any credibility. He goes on to say, I quote: “But if an offer of autonomy is mainly a façade it will not work, but if the majority groups and now I’m speaking globally of all countries, if governments are willing to give genuine autonomy to distinct groups that can go a long way, but it has to be a genuine offer, and it has to be an offer supported by the people of the majority group as well, not just the political parties.” At this point of time, Madam, I have not the slightest doubt in my mind that the vast majority of the Sinhala people in this country are prepared to give the Tamil people a reasonable solution. I am not prepared to be guided by the thinking of some ultra-nationalist groups that have managed to come to this House in recent times. The majority - the Government - the SLFP - and the UNP can come together and if there is genuine autonomy, there can be a solution to the conflict in this country, which will be accepted by both the Sinhalese people and the Tamil people. Therefore, before I conclude I want to make a final appeal to you: instead of trying your dirty tricks - stop this game of playing dirty tricks, come clean, be candid, be honest, be genuine, be straightforward - come up with a solution that would really be a solution to this conflict which has caused much human suffering to all people in this country. I thank you, Madam. * සභා ෙම්සය මත තබන ලද ලිපිය : சபாபீடத்தில் ைவக்கப்பட்ட கᾊதம் : Letter tabled :

XXV

Our disappointment with proposals contained in

the two Bills

28th Oct. ‘87 Shri RAJIV GANDHI, Prime Minister of India, NEW DHLHI. Dear Prime Minister,

We thank you once again for all four efforts on behalf of the Tamil people. We repeat our deep anguish at the tragic turn of events in Jaffna.

We feel it our duty to also express our disappointment with the proposals to solve the Tamil problem contained in the two Bills-the 13th. Amendment to the constitution and the provincial Councils Bill-

presented to Parliament by the Sri-Lankan Government. These proposals do not meet the aspirations of the Tamil people nor in any way, commensurate with the loss of life, sufferings and privations suffered by the Tamil people. Since 1983, the T.U.L.F., has always negotiated with the Government of Sri Lanka directly, utilizing the good offices of the Government of India, and through the Government of India in the hope of evolving a comprehensive scheme of devolution which the T.U.L.F. could commend to the Tamil people.

The T.U.L.F. regrets it cannot recommend the contents of these Bills to the Tamil people as being satisfactory, just and durable.

On the eve of your departure to Sri Lanka to sign the Agreement, we requested you among other things, that a team of experts from India along with their counterparts from Sri Lanka draft the necessary legislation. You agreed that this was a reasonable request.

Now the legislation is sought to be foisted on us without any India expert playing a part in the drafting.

The T.U.L.F. expected all along that a copy of the draft legislation would be made available to the Government of India at some reasonable time before it was made public. Apprehending that this might not happen, a delegation of the T.U.L.F. met President Jayewardene on the 29th of September 1987 and made this formal request. We regret that the Bills were gazetted without being made available to the Government of India.

This is not merely cavalier treatment of India but a clear breach of para 2.15 of the Agreement which states inter-alia that “residual matters shall be resolved between India and Sri Lanka”. The Bills are certainly not the result of any such resolution.

We do not wish to burden you with a detailed analysis of the Bills. But please permit us to draw your attention to some important matters.

1. Single Administrative Unit.

After a great deal of persuasion, you got President Jayewardene to agree to one administrative unit of the Northern and Eastern provinces as now constituted having one elected Provincial Council, one Governor, one Chief Minister and one Board of Ministers. The continuance of such a unit was to be subject to a referendum in the Eastern Province by 31st December 1988, which could be postponed by the President. We objected to such a referendum and we believed that it would eventually never be held.

The provisions of the Bills have made this political arrangement of such importance to the Tamils a farce. The setting up of a single administrative unit is to be done by an executive act of the President, in the form of a mere proclamation, which can always be revoked, and this too has to depend on the President being satisfied on a number of imponderables.

It was the Tamil expectation that a single administrative unit of the Northern and Eastern Provinces, would be firmly created by an adequate constitutional Provision. The Provision in Section 154 of the 13th Amendment, however, is of a dubious nature, and could be interpreted to

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 729 730

mean that a perpetual power is vested in Parliament to legislate on this all important matter. The resulting position would be that a single administrative unit of the Northern and Eastern Provinces, even when finally established would be an impermanent arrangement. 2. Legislative and Executive Power All parties to the negotiations have always understood that the powers to be devolved to the Provincial Council will be the same as those enjoyed by a State in India with suitable adaptations. This was to be particularly so in the field of legislative and executive power. During the discussions between the Sri Lankan Government and the T. U. L. F. in July/August 1986, it was agreed that the Legislative Power of the Province in respect of Provincial subjects would be near absolute, and that the Governor would be a ceremonial head, with his discretionary powers clearly defined. The Bills retain the power of Parliament to amend or repeal the chapter pertaining to Provincial Councils, and the Lists of Subjects, and also the power of Parliament to legislate even on subjects transferred to Provincial Councils, by a 2/3 rds. Majority, and the approval of the people of the whole country at a referendum. This would indeed be a simple exercise in Sri Lanka, where the majority community constitutes 74% of the population. In the field of executive power, the Executive Power of the President is sought to be retained by providing that the Governor shall hold office in accordance with Article 4(b), which provides that executive power of the people shall be exercised by the President of the Republic, through the wide and undefined discretionary powers of the Governor, which according to Section 154F (2) have to be exercised on the President’s directions; and through powers exercisable on the Proclamation of an emergency on very wide grounds. It would be relevant to recall that between 1970 and 1987, Sri Lanka has been under Emergency Rule for more than ten years. The Sri Lankan Government has declined to accept the T. U. L. F.’s persistent demand that the Indian pattern pertaining to the proclamation of emergency be followed. Not merely have the justiciablity of Proclamations of Emergency and Break down of Constitutional Machinery been specifically denied, power has even been vested with the President, to make Emergency Regulations with respect to any matter set out in the Provincial Council List, or having the effect of overriding amending or suspending the operation of a statute made by the Provincial Council. Vide Article 155 (3A). These Provisions were never accepted by the T. U. L. F. - some of them were not even proposed to the T. U. L. F. and we are certain that these provisions have not been accepted by India. During discussions with the T. U. L. F., the Sri Lankan Government indicated that the number of Ministers of the Province should not exceed one-third the total number of members. The North Eastern Province would have seventy one members. The T. U. L. F.’s proposal was that the number of Ministers should not exceed one-fifth the total number of Members. The number of Ministers has now been restricted to four. This has been done with the ulterior motive of promoting discord amongst the different peoples of the Northern and Eastern Provinces, and so as to diminish the importance of the Provincial Council and hamper and impede efficient Provincial Government.

3. Lists of Subjects Though it was clearly understood that the lists of Subjects would substantially conform to the Indian pattern, the Concurrent List has been heavily loaded, and the Provincial List clearly starved. Subjects such as Fisheries other than beyond Territorial Waters, Agriculture, Animal Husbandry, Industries, Redemarcation including creation of Districts,

Assistant Government Agents Divisions, and Grama Sevaka Divisions Restoration, reconstruction of destroyed towns. Villages, properties, compensation or relief to persons who have sustained loss or damage Palmyrah plantation and Palmyrah Industry, coconut plantation and industry related thereto, the ownership management and control of State-owned industrial enterprises within the Province dependant wholly or mainly on raw materials found in the Province (recommended by the Political Parties Conference) Co-operative Banks, Prisons, Provincial Public Service, Provincial Public Services Commission, Local Government . Nice, Inquiries, Surveys and Statistices for any of the purposes in the Provincial List and such others have not been included in the Provincial list, in keeping with the discussions held with the T. U. L. F. on the basis of the Indian pattern. In the field on Education, the powers of the Provincial Council are substantially curtailed even in the matter of secondary Education. Both the Conscurrent and Reserve lists have been so framed as to minimize to the maximum possible extent, the scope and content of the Provincial Council’s powers. 4. Land and land Settlement On the all important subject of Land and land Settlement, Appendix - II in the Bill is in many respects even worse than the Appendix attached to the proposals of 23rd September 1986 which itself was substantially deficient. The following matters are clearly unacceptable :- (i) The inclusion of State Land in the Reserve List, (ii) The reference to State Land continuing to be vested in the Republic, and the power of disposition by the President, (iii) The denial of the right to the Province, though land is a devolved subject, of the ipso-facto use of State Land for devolved subjects, (iv) The restriction of the right of the Province to administer and control only such land as is made available to it, (v) The stipulation that the alienation and disposition of State Land within a Province to any citizen or organization shall be by the President in accordance with “Laws” governing the matter contrary to even existing procedures for alienation, (vi) The wide definition given to Inter Provincial Irrigation and Land Development Projects, the principle of the National Ethnic Ratio in such projects, the right given to the Government of Sri Lanka to determine the selection of allottees for such lands, designedly to perpetuate the present pernicious practices, (vii) The failure to properly formulate the principle of the Cumulative Entitlement of the Tamil speaking people in Schemes under the Mahaweli Project in the Eastern Province, and the failure to Incorporate with Appendix - II the Annexure on settlement in the Eastern Province under the Mahaweli Project. The above are clearly directed towards reducing the Provincial Council to the position of a Nonentity in respect of State Land even though Land is a developed subject, and enabling the Central Government to have dominant power over State land. Ample scope is also retained for the continued colonization of the Northern and Eastern Provinces with members of the majority community. Such a position would be completely contrary to the discussions held with the T. U. L. F. and is totally different from the Indian pattern where Land Colonization etc., is a State subject with no power whatever reserved to the Union. The Tamils can never accept any settlement which does not satisfactorily resolve the burning question of State Land. The Land Settlement programmes carried out by the Sri Lankan Government in the post Agreement period have been a major destabilizing factor and do not inspire any confidence whatever in the Tamils.

2008 ෙපබරවාරි 06 731 732

5. Trincomalee Port The subject of Ports has been included in the reserve list and the Trincomalee Port as a Major Port would come under central control. Annexure “C” specifically provided that “A Port Authority under the Central Government will be set up for administrating the Trincomalee Port and Harbour. The area which will come under the administration of the Port Authority as well as the powers to be assigned to it will be further discussed.” This matter was raised with the Sri Lanka Government and though apparently certain assurances were given the Bills do not contain any provision reflecting such assurances. Tamil apprehensions are greatly aggravated by the fact that in 1984 after the finalization of Annexure “C” an extent of 5150 acres of land around the Trincomalee Port was vested in the Port Authority, which could result in the creation of a new Township with racial overtones around the Port, and be the cause for prolonged conflict. The manner of recruitment to employment in the Port since 1983 and the facilities provided to such employees clearly indicate this trend. The T. U. L. F. had given the Indian negotiators comprehensive paper dealing with this subject. It is essential that this matter too be resolved in an acceptable manner. 6. Provincial Public Service.

The provisions in respect to the Provincial Public Service and the Provincial Public Service Commission have been included in the Provincial Councils Bill contrary to the Sri Lankan Government’s draft proposals for the amendment of the constitution of 23rd September 1986 which categorically stated “Provision regarding Provincial Public Service to be included.” The appointment, transfer, dismissal and disciplinary control of Provincial Public Servants being vested in the Governor who is subject to Presidential directions is contrary to the proposal made by the T.U.L.F. that the provisions of Article 55 which vests the appointment, transfer, dismissal and disciplinary control of Public Officers in the Cabinet of Ministers be made mutatis - mutandis applicable. This together with the omission of the subjects of the Provincial Public Service and the Provincial Public Service Commission from the Provincial List, suggest that the Provincial Public Service will not function under the executive control of the Provincial Board of Ministers. Effective Provincial Government would be an impossibility in this situation. Contrary to the belief that the chapter pertaining to Provincial Councils would confer on the Provinces a measure of credible sutonomy without derogating from the entrenched clauses in the constitution, the present Bills at every turn, enable Parliament and the Central Executive, to extend its tentacles into the Provincial sphere circumscribing and emasculating the exercise of even the powers conferred on the Province. 7. Tamil as official Language and matters relating to the Central Government. The provisions in Clause 2 of the 13th Amendment making tamil also an Official Language has been nullified by paragraph (4) which states that “Parliament shall by law provide for the implementation of the provisions of this Chapter.” In relation to Sinhala as the Official Language, the Constitution provides for the manner of its use. The same constitutional provisions should be made applicable to tamil also as an official Language. Besides these there are other matters regarding the rights of the Tamils in relation to the Central Government which have to be discussed and resolved. In view of the above we earnestly request you to ask President Jayewardene not to proceed with the two Bills in Parliament in the present form till the matters referred to herein, are discussed and resolved to the satisfaction of the Tamil people. We request that we be granted an early appointment to discuss these matters more fully with you.

With kind regards,

Yours Sincerely, (Sgd) M.SIVASITHAMPARAM. (Sgd.) A. AMIRTHALINGUM. President, Secretary General, T.U.L.F. T.U.L.F. (Sgd) R. SAMPANTHAN, Vice - President, T.U.L.F., Former M. P. for Trincomalee.

[අ.භා. 12.12 ]

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (විෙද්ශ කටයුතු අමාතɕතුමා)

(மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம - ெவளிநாட்டᾤ வல்கள் அைமச்சர்)

(The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama - Minister of Foreign Affairs)

Madam Chairperson, I consider it a great pleasure to speak on the Emergency Debate at a time when we are confronted on one side, with an escalation of targeting civilians in our country by the terrorists and on the other, when we have announced political proposals that could address this national question.

The Hon. R. Sampanthan took great pains to explain this issue. I did listen to the Hon. Member’s lengthy speech. In a way, it was encouraging to note that today a dialogue has got started however much there is dissatisfaction. There is still hope that by having a dialogue, we could address the fundamental issues that have been confronting us.

The Government of Sri Lanka, led by President Rajapaksa, has made a beginning towards addressing the national question, which has protracted over several decades and on which the late President Jayewardene, in spite of having a five-sixths majority in the House, failed to fully implement the Constitution in a pragmatic manner.

ගරු ආර්. සම්පන්දන් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ஆர். சம்பந்தன்) (The Hon. R. Sampanthan)

Why did you break the MoU with the UNP? ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama)

You wait. I did not disturb you.

ගරු ආර්. සම්පන්දන් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ஆர். சம்பந்தன்) (The Hon. R. Sampanthan)

If you did not break the MoU with the UNP, you would have had a two - thirds majority in Parliament.

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama)

From when have you started speaking for the UNP? ගරු ආර්. සම්පන්දන් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ஆர். சம்பந்தன்) (The Hon. R. Sampanthan)

Why did you break that MoU? ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama)

I will come to the bare facts. Let me respond, Hon. Member. The MoU between the UNP and the SLFP, the main constituent party in the Government led by President

5 — PL 002898 — (2008/03)

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 733 734

Rajapaksa, is independent of all these issues. If the UNP is willing to support this process, they are always welcome to do so. Our Government has opened doors for everybody, including the TNA, to come on board to address this issue in a practical and pragmatic manner. Dogmatism is something we have to say, "no" to.

ගරු සුෙර්ෂ් ෙපේමචන්දන් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு சுேரஷ் பிேரமச்சந்திரன்) (The Hon. Suresh Premachandran)

They did not invite us for the APRC.

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama)

Okay. ගරු සුෙර්ෂ් ෙපේමචන්දන් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு சுேரஷ் பிேரமச்சந்திரன்) (The Hon. Suresh Premachandran) The President never invited the TNA for the APRC. Do you know that?

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) We are always willing to do so. - [Interruption.] The APRC is still sitting. - [Interruption.]

මූලාසනාරූඪ මන්තීතුමිය (தைலைமதாங்கும் உᾠப்பினர் அவர்கள்) (The Presiding Member) Hon. Member, please do not disturb him. ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) Let me reply you. The APRC is still sitting; the APC is still there and you are welcome to be there tomorrow. I will communicate your willingness. - [Interruption.] You must come to the APC. Why are you not coming? Why are you not making your submissions known and why do you not want to be a part of the solution rather than a part of the problem? We do not want to hear the LTTE's voice in this Chamber in terms of -

ගරු සුෙර්ෂ් ෙපේමචන්දන් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு சுேரஷ் பிேரமச்சந்திரன்) (The Hon. Suresh Premachandran) Ha, ha! ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) I know your restrictions; I know your limitations. - [Interruption.] I know you are being led not by the people's will - [Interruption.] I am posing this question to you. - [Interruption.] You are being led by the fascist terrorists who are dictating to you.

ගරු සුෙර්ෂ් ෙපේමචන්දන් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு சுேரஷ் பிேரமச்சந்திரன்) (The Hon. Suresh Premachandran) You answer the questions raised by the Hon. Sampanthan.

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) Every time we come out with a solution, this happens. - [Interruption.] How can we satisfy the blood-thirst of the LTTE? - [Interruption.] Hon. Presiding Member, I will be taking more time from the Opposition.

මූලාසනාරූඪ මන්තීතුමිය (தைலைமதாங்கும் உᾠப்பினர் அவர்கள்) (The Presiding Member) Hon. Member, please allow the Hon. Minister to speak. ගරු සුෙර්ෂ් ෙපේමචන්දන් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு சுேரஷ் பிேரமச்சந்திரன்) (The Hon. Suresh Premachandran) Why do not answer the questions? ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) I am answering the questions. One question was, why were you not invited for the APC? Right now, the Government is willing to invite the TNA to be a part of the APC. - [Interruption.] Come and present your submissions to the APC. After all, this is part of democracy. - [Interruption.]

ගරු මන්තීවරෙයක් (மாண்ᾗமிகு உᾠப்பினர் ஒᾞவர்) (An Hon. Member) The LTTE will not allow them to come. ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) You come and show us what your proposals are. - [Interruption.]

මූලාසනාරූඪ මන්තීතුමිය (தைலைமதாங்கும் உᾠப்பினர் அவர்கள்) (The Presiding Member) ගරු ඇමතිතුමනි, ඔබතුමා මූලාසනයට කථා කරන්න. එතෙකොට පශ්න මතු වන එකක් නැහැ.

ගරු ආර්. සම්පන්දන් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ஆர். சம்பந்தன்) (The Hon. R. Sampanthan) Your Government comes up with the proposal of a unitary Constitution with the district as the unit of devolution and insists on that position. Today you have virtually come up with something called the Thirteenth Amendment, which is twenty years old and now you want us to come to the APRC. Are we a bunch of donkeys to come there?

[ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා]

2008 ෙපබරවාරි 06 735 736

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) Let me answer. Hon. Member, as far as you are not a part of the Tigers, you can always be a part of this process.- [Interruption.] A donkey is more respectable. That is more decent than the blood-thirsty Tigers.

Having said that, I will continue to respond to the Hon. Sampanthan because he articulated where the Government has failed; where President Jayewardene and the subsequent Governments in power for the last twenty years failed. That was the crux of his submission before the House this morning. I welcome that because the history must be spoken about. Otherwise, we would not learn lessons from past experiences for the present and the future. What did our President when addressing the APC at the time of the handing over of the APRC Proposals say? He said, "The political issues have to be addressed politically and this is the beginning of that process". This is the beginning of that process. The APRC has not stopped its deliberations. They continued to hold two subsequent meetings after handing over the APRC Proposals for the full implementation of the Constitution. Do you expect a newly-born infant to walk before he could crawl? Twenty years have passed since that Amendment got into the Constitution of our country. There was no political will or political direction for its proper implementation. Why are we hiding behind the myth that we can deliver something more substantial? Is the House in agreement to implement whatever we decide in terms of our own expectations, the expectations of this country? There are stages one has to go by and the process has to take its course. That is the course we have taken with practicality and pragmatism in a pluralistic, democratic society.

It is unfortunate that today two districts are being dictated by terrorists who have no respect for human life. Children going to school, children going for sports have to lay their lives because there is this madness in the country with suicide cadres mobilized by the LTTE seeking a fascist regime. Who is speaking for those children? Would anyone stand up for them? It is sad when it happens. Even the UNP is not ready to vote for the extension of the Emergency. Abstaining is the easiest thing to do. Here is a country that needs salvation, liberation from the terrorist clutches. Scourge of terrorism has gone on too long in this country and I am happy to state today that the international community has come together to endorse the proposals that we have presented. I and Mr. Richard Boucher, the Under-Secretary, spoke on the 4th over the telephone. I must be happy to state here now that I am responding because you named Mr. Boucher, the Under-Secretary of the United States State Department, by name. And, what did he say? He said, “This is a good beginning and make it happen.” Yes, that is what we are going to make happen. And we are going to implement it, rather than being jittery, what we have got in our hands. This is where every

consecutive government failed. You could not find answers why governments previously failed though you said so. There were more expectations that you generated out of President Jayewardene. Yes, people can make submissions; people can listen to submissions; people can agree with the submissions but there is the divide in terms of implementation against acceptance. This is what has happened. This is where the TNA failed; the TULF failed in spite of all your great efforts and your leadership. We did value the efforts of the Tamil leadership in our country. In a pluralistic society we can always discard what we cannot agree with because there has to be pluralistic democratic traditions and principles that we are all committed to as enshrined in our Constitution. It is from that angle that we are looking at it.

Today, some may say that the LTTE is now escalating violence because there is no CFA in force. As the Foreign Minister of Sri Lanka I must ask, "Were there no violations when the CFA was in force? How many people had to lay down their lives because of the terrorists attacks? Did the Dambulla attack on the bus, the Nugegoda attack, the Slave Island attack, the Kebithigollewa attack I and II and all other attacks that targeted the civilians of our country take place after the annulment of the CFA or before? The answer to that is, the LTTE’s frustration getting escalated due to the successes of the military because today we are attacking the targets of the LTTE not the civilians like what happened in the past. We are very careful to see that the sovereignty and the territorial integrity of the country is protected through professionally-handled military operations in the conflict areas. We have to disarm the people who are carrying arms. We have to get the essence of the democracy established in all parts of our country. Today the frustration of the LTTE is that we have overtaken the LTTE in terms of democratic approaches; the political issues have now surfaced and they are being addressed by the Government of Sri Lanka through political means. And that is how the APRC Proposals came out, and India along with the other countries have come to endorse it as the beginning of the right direction for the country to move. That is the beginning and that is the right direction. That is why the LTTE is getting further frustrated and isolated in the international community and amongst their own community in Sri Lanka.

The LTTE diaspora, the Tamil diaspora who believed in a reasonable solution is being canvassed by the Government of Sri Lanka today and the Foreign Ministry is doing its best in order to penetrate the international Tamil diaspora with our communications to them and they are being well-received. In fact, today I am happy to state in this House that we have started sending communications from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to the Tamil population living both in Sri Lanka and abroad stating what we do and what we stand for as a country. This is what we termed as the re-launch of the “Nambikkai”. I will send you a copy of this

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 737 738

[ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා]

newsletter, Hon. Sampanthan. These are what we have to reach out to because the Tamil people are part of this country. The Tamils who live abroad are also part of this country. They are the ones who have been dictated and subjugated by the LTTE wherever they live. Their children have been made to be suicide cadres giving their lives for a fascist dictator, Prabhakaran who had terrorized this country and taken the terror across the shores of Sri Lanka, even to India, becoming the mercenary today in other locations where terrorism is fostering. This is the challenge we have taken upon ourselves; this is the challenge we are addressing. This is why we are inviting the TNA and I am glad that you have responded well. You have a role to play in the political process of our country. That role is very much there for the democratically-elected Members coming from the TNA. Do not be part of the dictation that comes from the LTTE. Do not be the voice of the LTTE. Be the voice of the Tamil community; be part of that agenda. That is why we have a respect for Mr. Anandasangaree. Why did he subscribe to the proposals that have come from the APRC? Why did he say this is a good beginning? Because he has studied all the proposals that came up for the last 30 years in this country unable being delivered. Here is a Government that has come to deliver. That is the difference between delivering and unable to deliver and causing frustration to the people of this country, not one community but all communities.

People today need peace, sustainable peace. This is not a gimmick to reach sustainable peace in our country. Why have we demonstrated in the Eastern Province of our country since its liberation numbering three districts? Today we have started the recruitment of the police from the Tamil-speaking people and the Tamil community. How many members have joined the recruitment drive of the police in the Eastern Province today? We want to empower the people of their security, their rights to be protected, in terms of their wherewithal, their properties, their livelihood, generation of income and above all, bring prosperity to all regions of our country.

Where was the distribution of Sri Lanka’s GDP concentrated? It concentrated in the South as the other locations were not accessible to people who wanted to go and make investment because the LTTE stopped that, prevented that. I know it so well having been the Minister of Industries five or six years ago. Still we could not take development to the Eastern and the Northern Provinces because of the LTTE's dictation that they did not want any development activities to take place in spite of the CFA signed by the then Prime Minister, the Hon. Ranil Wickremasinghe at that time. That was the dictation that came on us; they wanted to dictate to the people.

මූලාසනාරූඪ මන්තීතුමිය (தைலைமதாங்கும் உᾠப்பினர் அவர்கள்) (The Presiding Member) ගරු ඇමතිතුමනි, ඔබතුමාට ෙවන් කර තිෙබන කාලය අවසානයි.

ගරු ෙරෝහිත ෙබෝෙගොල්ලාගම මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ேராஹித ேபாெகால்லாகம) (The Hon. Rohitha Bogollagama) මූලාසනාරූඪ ගරු මන්තීතුමියනි, මට තවත් විනාඩි ෙදකක් ෙදන්න.

That is the process that we are following and want everyone in the polity of Sri Lanka to be part of, and the international community is watching this development with great expectation and hope; the hope being that for the first time the Government of Sri Lanka has been able to deliver something that has got into our Constitution but unable to be implemented. To deliver what is unable to be implemented is a new beginning. Once again I state that what has got into our Constitution that has been jointly formulated is what we have to address with pragmatism.

Terrorism has to be countered and President Mahinda Rajapaksa went on to state that terrorism has to be countered whilst addressing political issues politically. This is the process that we follow and our two-pronged approach for Sri Lanka in the year 2008 is aimed at achieving security for our people and this is where we need the condemnation of the LTTE for all the atrocities that they are committing on the lives of our people. When the corpses of the children are brought to their homes, what kind of a pathetic state are the households in all parts of Sri Lanka plunged into? This is the answer that we have to jointly find. This is the process that we have to advocate in terms of getting support from all quarters of Sri Lanka towards the proper implementation of this process.

Once we hold elections in the Eastern Province, another proposal will come from the APRC. Proposals have to be implemented and elections are to be won. Shortly there will be elections in the Eastern Province that will enshrine what we have said here and the implementation process will begin. It is important that we come together in this drive. Divided, you are only supporting the LTTE and I know that all the respectable Members of the TNA will be part of this drive in order to support your people, the people who have great expectations of you and not the fascist terrorists who have a thirst for a separatist movement purely for the survival of their operations and thrive for further atrocities and brutality towards the civilized society of Sri Lanka. Therefore, I think all parties across the Divide must join and support the Government at this endeavour to realize the expectations of our people.

Thank you, Madam.

මූලාසනාරූඪ මන්තීතුමිය (தைலைமதாங்கும் உᾠப்பினர் அவர்கள்) (The Presiding Member) ගරු පත්ම උදයශාන්ත ගුණෙසේකර මන්තීතුමා.

2008 ෙපබරවාරි 06 739 740

[අ.භා. 12.31] ගරු ආර්. එම්. පත්ම උදයශාන්ත ගුණෙසේකර මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ஆர். எம். பத்ம உதயஷாந்த குணேசகர) (The Hon. R.M. Padma Udayashantha Gunasekera) මූලාසනාරූඪ ගරු මන්තීතුමියනි, අද දිනෙය් දී හදිසි නීතිය යටෙත් ඉදිරිපත් කර ඇති ෙයෝජනාව සම්මත කර ගැනීමට අදාළ ෙම් විවාදෙය් දී විෙශේෂෙයන්ම මෙග් පැත්ෙතන් කරුණු කිහිපයක් ඉදිරිපත් කරන්න මා සූදානම්. කුරිරු එල්ටීටීඊ තස්තවාදීන් විසින් රට තුළ සිදු කරන ලද, ඉතාම අවාසනාවන්ත සිදුවීම් ගණනාවක් පසු ගිය දින කීපය තුළ වාර්තා වුණා. විෙශේෂෙයන්ම ෙකොළඹ ෙකොටුෙව් සිදු කරපු සාහසික මිනිස් ඝාතනය හරහා ඉතා වටිනා ජීවිත පමාණයක් අෙප් දැයට අද දවෙසේ අහිමි කර තිෙබනවා. ඒ අය අතර පාසල් ශිෂɕ ශිෂɕාවන් කිහිප ෙදෙනක් සිටිනවා. ඒ අතෙර් ෙදමළ ජාතික ශිෂɕ සෙහෝදරයකුත් සිටිනවා.

ඒ වෙග්ම පසු ගිය දිනවල වාර්තා වුණු දඹුල්ෙල් බස් ෙබෝම්බය නිසා, පිච්ච මල් පූජාවකට අනුරාධපුර නගරය බලා ගිය සැදැහැවතුන් පිරිසක් ඉතාම කුරිරු ෙලස ඝාතනයට ලක් වුණා. ඒ වෙග්ම වැලිඔය ජානකපුර දී ක්ෙල්ෙමෝ පහාරයකට ලක් කරලා එතැනදීත් මිනිස් ජීවිත ගණනාවක් බිලි ගත්තා. පසු ගිය දිනයක ෙමොනරාගල දිස්තික්කෙය්, බුත්තල, ෙහළගම පෙද්ශෙය් දී එල්ල කළ ක්ෙල්ෙමෝ පහාරය නිසාත්, ඒ වෙග්ම ඒ ෙමොෙහොෙත් සිදු කළ ෙවඩි තැබීම හරහාත් මිනිස් ජීවිත ගණනාවක් බිලි ගත්තා. එදා දිනෙය්ම ෙමොනරාගල දිස්තික්කෙය්, බුත්තල, ඔක්කම්පිටිය, දෙඹ්යාය, නුගමණ්ඩිය පෙද්ශෙය් අහිංසක ෙහේන් ෙගොවීන් පිරිසක් එල්ටීටීඊ තස්තවාදීන් විසින් ඝාතනය කළා. ඊට දින ෙදකකට විතර පසුව තණමල්විල පාෙද්ශීය ෙල්කම් ෙකොට්ඨාසෙය් හම්ෙබ්ගමුව, කලවැල්ගල පෙද්ශෙය්දී ඉතාමත් අසරණ අහිංසක ෙහේන් ෙගොවීන් පිරිසක් ඇතුළුව සාහසික මිනිස් ඝාතන සිදු කළා. ෙම් ආදී වශෙයන් එල්ටීටීඊ තස්තවාදීන් විසින් රට පුරා විවිධ තැන්වල, දකුෙණ් විවිධ තැන්වල මිනිස් ෙබෝම්බ අටවමින්, මරා ෙගන මැෙරන ෙබෝම්බකරුවන් එවමින්, ක්ෙල්ෙමෝ ෙබෝම්බ පහාර සිදු කරමින්, අහිංසක මිනිස් ජීවිත ගණනාවක් බිලි අර ෙගන තිෙබනවා. ඒ අතෙර් අෙප් රෙට් පභූවරුන් කිහිප ෙදනකුටත් මරා ෙගන මැෙරන ෙබෝම්බ පහාරයන් එල්ල කිරීමට සූදානම් වුණු අවස්ථා තිබුණා.

ඒ වෙග්ම වත්තල පෙද්ශෙය් දී මරා ෙගන මැෙරන ඇඳුම් කට්ටල ගණනාවක් හමු වුණා. ඒ වෙග්ම රාජɕ ෙනොවන සංවිධාන මැදිහත් වීෙමන් එල්ටීටීඊ තස්තවාදීන් ෙවත සැපයීමට සූදානම් කළ ෙවඩි ෙනොවදින ඇඳුම් කට්ටල ගණනාවක් මැදවච්චිය ෙපොලිස් මාර්ග බාධකෙය්දී අත් අඩංගුවට ගත්තා. ෙසොලිඩා කියන රාජɕ ෙනොවන සංවිධානය සතුව අනුරාධපුර නගරෙය් පිහිටි ගබඩාවක එවැනි ෙවඩි ෙනොවදින ඇඳුම් ෙදසිය ගණනක් සමඟ ඇඳුම් කට්ටල ගණනාවක් හසු වුණා. ඒ වෙග්ම ෙලෝක ආහාර වැඩසටහන යටෙත් යුනිෙසෆ් සංවිධානය මැදිහත් ෙවලා කූට ෙලස ෙගන්වන ලද, වɕාජ ෙලස ෙගන්වන ලද, යාපනය බලා එල්ටීටීඊ තස්තවාදීන් ෙවත රැෙගන යමින් තිබූ අධි ෙපෝෂිත බිස්කට් වර්ග ගණනාවක් හමු වුණා. ඒවා අත් අඩංගුවට ගත්තා. ෙම් ආදී වශෙයන් කරුණු ගණනාවක් එකට ෙපළ ගැසී තිෙබනවා. එල්ටීටීඊ සංවිධානය දකුණු පෙද්ශය සහ ෙම් පෙද්ශය ඉලක්ක කර ගනිමින්, තස්තවාදී කටයුතු පමාණයක් ෙම් ෙමොෙහොෙත් සිදු කරමින් සිටිනවා.

ඉතාම පැහැදිලිවම ගත්තාට පස්ෙසේ, ෙම් සිදුවීම් ගණනාව හරහා එල්ටීටීඊ තස්තවාදීන් අරමුණු කරන කරුණු ගණනාවක් තිෙබනවා. ෙමය, තිවිධ හමුදාව උතුෙර් ඉතා දැවැන්ත ෙමෙහයුමක ෙයදී සිටිමින්, උතුෙර් ෙකොටි තස්තවාදීන් ඉතාම දරුණු පරාජයකට ලක් කරමින් සිටින ෙවලාවක් බව අපි දන්නවා. එල්ටීටීඊ තස්තවාදීන් පසු ගිය කාලෙය් දී උතුෙර්දී වෙග්ම නැ ෙඟනහිර පෙද්ශ ගණනාවකම දිගින් දිගටම දැවැන්ත ෙලස පරාජය වුණා. එල්ටීටීඊ තස්තවාදීන් යුදමය ෙලස පරාජය කරන්න බැහැයි කියලා රට ඇතුෙළේ මතයක් හදලා තිබුණා.

"යුද්ධෙයන් දිනන්න බැහැ. ෙකොටින්ට ගහන්න බැහැ. ෙකොටි යුදමය ෙලස පරාජය කරන්න බැහැ" කියලා රෙට් මතයක් හදලා තිබුණා. දකුෙණ් සමහර ෙද්ශපාලන වɕාපාර විසින්, සමහර පුද්ගලයන් විසින්, එල්ටීටීඊ මතය ෙවනුෙවන් ෙපනී සිටින සමහර රාජɕ ෙනොවන සංවිධාන විසින්, ෙද්ශපාලන ෙයෝජනාවලි ෙගෙනන සමහර රාජɕ ෙනොවන සංවිධාන විසින් එවැනි මතයක් රෙට් හදලා තිබුණා. නමුත්, ෙම් ෙමොෙහොෙත් ඒ මතය පරාජය කර තිෙබනවා. අෙප් රෙට් ගුවන් හමුදාව, පා බළ හමුදාව, නාවික හමුදාව ඇතුළු අෙප් රෙට් ආරක්ෂක අංශ විසින් එල්ටීටීඊ සංවිධානය යුදමය ෙලස පරාජය කරන්න පුළුවන්ය කියන මතය රටට තහවුරු කර දී තිෙබනවා. අද වන්නිෙය් මහා ෙමෙහයුමක් සිදු කරමින් තිෙබනවා. ඒ සඳහා මුළු රෙට්, ජාතිෙය් අවධානය ෙයොමු ෙවලා තිෙබන ෙවලාවක්. සියලු ෙදනාෙග්ම ආශීර්වාදය, ෛධර්යය, ශක්තිය ඒ ෙවත ෙයොමු ෙවලා තිෙබන ෙවලාවක්, ෙම්. රෙට් සැෙවොම එකාවන්ව, යුදමය ෙලස ෙකොටි තස්තවාදය පරාජය කිරීෙම් කටයුත්ත දිහා ඉතාමත් අවධානෙයන්, වුවමනාෙවන් බලා සිටින ෙවලාවක් ෙම්. ඒ නිසා ෙම් ෙවලාෙව් දකුෙණ් සිද්ධ කරන තස්ත කියා මාර්ග හරහා දකුණ භීතියකට පත් කරලා, දකුෙණ් ජන ජීවිතය කලබලයකට පත් කරලා, දකුෙණ් ජන ජීවිතය අසහනයකට පත් කරලා, දකුණ අස්ථාවර කරලා, උතුෙර් ෙමෙහයුම් අඩාළ කිරීෙම් පථම වුවමනාව ඉටු කර ගැනීමට ෙකොටි තස්තවාදීන්ට වුවමනා ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ෙකොටි තස්තවාදීන් තමන්ෙග් යුද ඉතිහාසය තුළ, ෙබදුම්වාදී වුවමනාව ෙවනුෙවන් ඉතිහාසය පුරාම කරන ලද කාර්යය ඒකයි. ෙකොටින් යුදමය ෙලස අස්ථාවර වන විට, හැම ෙමොෙහොෙත්ම යුදමය ෙලස ෙකොටින් පරාජයට පත් වන විට ෙමන්න ෙම් කියා මාර්ගවලට ඔවුන් ඇවිත් තිෙබනවා. අනාරක්ෂිත ගම්මානවලට පැනලා අහිංසක සිවිල් ජනතාව කපා ෙකොටා මරා දැමූ ඉතිහාසයක් අප දන්නවා. ෙමොණරාගල, අම්පාර, අනුරාධපුරය, ෙපොෙළොන්නරුව, තිකුණාමලය, පුත්තලම, මන්නාරම වාෙග් දිස්තික්කවල පසු ගිය ඉතිහාසය තුළම ෙම්ක සිද්ධ වුණා. දැන් ඒ කියා මාර්ග නැවතත් ෙකොටි සංවිධානය පටන් අරෙගන තිෙබනවා. අනාරක්ෂිත ගම්මානවල විතරක් ෙනොෙවයි, දැන් රට ඇතුෙළේ දකුණු පෙද්ශෙය් විවිධ ගම්මානවලටත් ෙම්ක ඇවිත් තිෙබනවා. උදාහරණයක් විධියට අෙප් දිස්තික්කෙය් - ෙමොණරාගල දිස්තික්කෙය් - බුත්තල නගරෙය් සිට කිෙලෝමීටර් තුනකට ආසන්න ෙහළගම පෙද්ශෙය්දී තමයි ක්ෙල්ෙමෝ පහාරයක් එල්ල කෙළේ. මීට කලින් බුත්තල, නියදැල්ල, ඔක්කම්පිටිය වාෙග් පෙද්ශවලට 1991, 1998 වාෙග් වසරවලදී ෙකොටි තස්තවාදීන් පැමිණිලා එල්ල කරපු සමහර පහාරයන් දැන් බුත්තල නගරය ආසන්න පෙද්ශයට ඇවිත් තිෙබන්ෙන්, ඔවුන්ෙග් අන්න ඒ වුවමනාව හරහා දකුණ අස්ථාවර තත්ත්වයකට පත් කිරීෙම් වුවමනාෙවන්.

මුලසනාරූඪ ගරු මන්තීතුමියනි, දකුෙණ්, තණමල්විල පාෙද්ශීය ෙල්කම් ෙකොට්ඨාසෙය් කලවැල්ගල පෙද්ශෙයන් එහා පැත්ෙත් සීමාව තමයි බලංෙගොඩ, හපුතෙල්, බලහරුව සීමාව. බලහරුව සීමාෙවන් එහා පැත්ෙත් ෙකොස්ලන්ද සීමාව. ඒ දක්වා ෙකොටි තස්තවාදීන් ඇවිත් පහාර එල්ල කරන්ෙන් ඒ පෙද්ශවල ජනතාව තුළ මහා භීතියක් ඇති කරලා, ෙම් තස්තවාදය පරාජය කරන්න සිදු කරන කටයුතු - උතුෙර් සිදු කරන හමුදා ෙමෙහයුම් - අඩාළ කරලා දකුණ ෙවත හමුදාවෙග් ඇස ෙයොමු කර ගැනීෙම් වුවමනාෙවන්. ඒක තමයි ඔවුන්ට වුවමනා ෙවලා තිෙබන්ෙන්. උතුෙර් ඉන්න හමුදා ඛණ්ඩ දකුණට අද්දා ගැනීෙම් වුවමනාව ෙකොටින්ට ඇති ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ඒ නිසා දකුණ අස්ථාවර බවකට පත් කර ගැනීෙම් වුවමනාවක් ෙකොටින්ට ෙම් හරහා තිෙබනවා.

මූලාසනාරූඪ ගරු මන්තීතුමියනි, අනික් කාරණය ෙම්කයි. පසු ගිය කාලෙය්ම Tamilnet ෙවබ් අඩවිය - එල්ටීටීඊ තස්තවාදීන්ෙග් ෙවබ් අඩවි - හරහා ඔවුන් නිකුත් කරමින් හිටි පණිවුඩය අප දන්නවා. විෙශේෂෙයන් ෙකොටි මුලස්ථානවලට ගුවන් පහාර එල්ල ෙවද්දී, ඒ බංකර් සම්පූර්ණෙයන්ම සුනු විසුනු ෙවලා යද්දී, තමිල්ෙචල්වන් කියන ෙද්ශපාලන අංශෙය් නායකයා මිය යද්දී, ෙකොටි සංවිධානෙය් ඉන්න නායකත්වයන් විනාශ ෙවද්දී, ෙකොටි සංවිධානෙය් තිෙබන හමුදා ඛණ්ඩ විනාශ ෙවද්දී ඔවුන් ඒ ෙවබ් අඩවිවල පළ කරමින් හි ටිෙය් ෙමොකක්ද? ඔවුන් කියා තිබුණා

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 741 742

ජාතɕන්තර අවධානය දැන් රටට ෙයොමු වන්න ඕනෑය කියා. ඔවුන්ෙග් සමහර ෙවබ් අඩවිවල තිබුෙණ් ෙමොනවාද? ඇෙමරිකාව සුඩානයට මැදිහත් වනවා නම්, ඇෙමරිකාව ඉ රාකයට මැදිහත් වනවා නම්, ඇයි ලංකාවට මැදිහත් ෙනො වන්ෙන් කියා ඒ සන්නද්ධ අංශ නායකයන් පසිද්ධිෙය් තමන්ෙග් ෙවබ් අඩවිවලට පකාශ නිකුත් කර තිබුණා. ඔවුන් එයින් ෙමොකක්ද බලාෙපොෙරොත්තු වන්ෙන්? ජාතɕන්තර අවධානය - බටහිර අවධානය - දිනා ගන්න. එෙහම නැත්නම් එක්සත් ජාතීන්ෙග් සාම සාධක හමුදාවක් ලංකාවට ෙගන්වන තත්ත්වයක් ඇතුෙළේ අ ෙප් රට තව දුරටත් අරාජික තත්ත්වයට අර ෙගන ගිහින් ෙබදුම්වාදී දිසාවට, තස්තවාදෙය් වුවමනාෙව් දිසාවට ෙම් පශ්නය කැන්දා ෙගන යන සංකීර්ණ මට්ටම ට ෙගන යෑෙම් වුවමනාව තමයි අද එල්ටීටීඊ තස්තවාදීන්ට ඕනෑ ෙවලා තිෙබන්ෙන්. ඒ නිසා ෙම් කාරණය ඉතාමත් පැහැදිලියි.

ෙම් තත්ත්වය ඇතුෙළේ අප ඉතාමත් පැහැදිලිව රටක් හැටියට ඉ ටු කළ යුතු කාර්ය භාරය ෙමොකක්ද? අද උතුෙර් සිදු කරනු ලබන හමුදා ෙමෙහයුම් කිසි ෙසේත්ම අඩාළ කළ යුතු නැහැ. තස්තවාදය යුදමය ෙලස පරාජය කිරීෙම් කටයුත්තට අෙප් සම්පූර්ණ සහාය දීලා, තිවිධ හමුදාව ගනු ලබන සියලු කියා මාර්ග ඇතුෙළේ ෙම් රටට ෙගෞරවාන්විත සාමය රැෙගන ඒෙම් කටයුත්ත දිසාවට ඒ හමුදා ෙමෙහයුම් සිදු කරලා, එල්ටීටීඊ තස්තවාදය යුදමය ෙලස සහමුලින් පරාජය කිරීෙම් කටයුත්ත අද රෙට්, ජාතිෙය් පමුඛ කාර්යභාරය බවට පත් ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. එය ෙනොපිරිෙහළා ඉ ටු කරන්න ඕනෑකම තිෙබනවා. අප දන්නවා ෙම් ෙමොෙහොත වන විට සර්ව පාර්ශ්වික ෙයෝජනා, ෙබදුම්වාදී ෙයෝජනා රැෙගන ඇවිත් තිෙබන බව. නැවතත් තස්තවාදය යුදමය ෙලස -

මූලාසනාරූඪ මන්තීතුමිය (தைலைமதாங்கும் உᾠப்பினர் அவர்கள்) (The Presiding Member) ගරු මන්තීතුමනි, මඳක් නිහඬ වන්න. ෙම් අවස්ථාෙව්දී මූලාසනය සඳහා ගරු වී. පුත්තිරසිගාමනී මන්තීතුමාෙග් නම ෙයෝජනා කරන්න.

ගරු ගාමිණී ෙලොකුෙග් මහතා (කීඩා හා ෙපොදු විෙනෝදාත්මක කටයුතු අමාතɕතුමා)

(மாண்ᾗமிகு காமினி ெலாக்குேக - விைளயாட்ᾌத்ᾐைற, ெபாᾐப் ெபாᾨᾐேபாக்கு அᾤவல்கள் அைமச்சர்)

(The Hon. Gamini Lokuge - Minister of Sports and Public Recreation)

"ගරු වී. පුත්තිරසිගාමනී මහතා දැන් මූලාසනය ගත යුතුය" යි මා ෙයෝජනා කරනවා.

පශ්නය විමසන ලදින්, සභා සම්මත විය. வினா விᾌக்கப்பட்ᾌ ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்ளப்பட்டᾐ. Question put, and agreed to. අනතුරුව ගරු ෙර්ණුකා ෙහේරත් මහත්මිය මූලාසනෙයන් ඉවත් වූෙයන්, ගරු වී. පුත්තිරසිගාමනී මහතා මූලාසනාරූඪ විය.

அதன்பிறகு, மாண்ᾗமிகு (திᾞமதி) ேரᾎகா ேஹரத் அவர்கள் அக்கிராசனத்தினின்ᾠ அகலேவ, மாண்ᾗமிகு ᾪ. ᾗத்திரசிகாமணி அவர்கள் தைலைம வகித்தார்கள்.

Whereupon THE HON. (MRS.) RENUKA HERATH left the Chair, and THE HON. V. PUTHTHIRASIGAMONEY took the Chair.

ගරු ආර්. එම්. පත්ම උදයශාන්ත ගුණෙසේකර මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ஆர். எம். பத்ம உதயஷாந்த குணேசகர) (The Hon. R.M. Padma Udayashantha Gunasekera) මූලාසනාරූඪ ගරු මන්තීතුමනි, මා කියමින් හිටිෙය් ෙම්කයි. ෙම් තස්තවාදය යුදමය වශෙයන් පරාජය කිරීෙම් කටයුත්ත තමයි, අද රට හමුෙව්, ජාතිය හමුෙව් තිෙබන කාර්යභාරය වන්ෙන්.

ෙදබිඩි පතිපත්තිවලින් යුදමය ෙලස තස්තවාදය පරාජය කරන්න පුළුවන්කමක් නැහැ. ෙබදුම්වාදය ශක්තිමත් කරන දිශාවට ෙයෝජනා සකස් කරලා, එය රට තුළ තහවුරු කරමින් යන ගමන හරහා සිදු වන්ෙන් නැවතත් පරණ සුපුරුදු ගමන් මාවතට ෙම් රට ෙසේන්දු වීමයි. නැවතත් ෙබදුම්වාදය ශක්තිමත් කිරීෙම් වැඩ ෙකොටස ඒ හරහා ඉටු වීමයි. ඒ නිසා, තස්තවාදය යුදමය ෙලස පරාජය කිරීම තමයි පථම, අංක එෙක් කාර්යය. එයින් පසුව ෙදමළ ජනතාවෙග් පශ්න, උතුෙර් සංවර්ධන ගැටලු, ෙදමළ ජනතාවෙග් පජාතන්තවාදී අයිතිවාසිකම්, ෙකොටි තස්තවාදෙය් මහා වහල් කඳවුෙර් හිර කර තිෙබන ෙදමළ ජනතාවෙග් අයිතිවාසිකම් ෙවනුෙවන් කටයුතු කරලා ඒවා ලබා දීෙම් කටයුත්ත රටක් හැටියට ඉටු කරන්න ඕනෑකම තිෙබනවා. තනි රටක් ඇතුෙළේ ඒ පශ්න විසඳන කියාමාර්ගයි, ගත යුතුව තිෙබන්ෙන්. අෙප් රෙට් ඒකීය බව රැක ගනිමින්, ස්ෛවරීත්වය රැක ගනිමින්, අෙප් රෙට් ෙගෞරවය රැක ගනිමින් ෙබදුම්වාදය පරාජය කරන, තස්තවාදයට උඩ ෙගඩි ෙනොෙදන කියාවලියකටයි ඒ විසඳුම් මාලාව සකස් කර ගන්න ඕනෑ. ඒ නිසා යුදමය ෙලස ෙකොටි තස්තවාදය පරාජය කිරීෙම් කටයුත්ත ෙකෙරහි තමයි ෙම් ෙමොෙහොෙත් අප අවධානය ෙයොමු කරන්න ඕනෑ ෙවන්ෙන්.

ඒ වාෙග්ම මූලාසනාරූඪ ගරු මන්තීතුමනි, අධිෙපෝෂණ බිස්කට් අරෙගන යමින්, ඒ වාෙග්ම ෙවඩි ෙනොවදින ඇඳුම් අරෙගන යමින් විවිධ කියාමාර්ග හරහා ෙම් ෙමොෙහො ෙත් රාජɕ ෙනොවන සංවිධාන මැදිහත් ෙවමින් ඉන්ෙන් ෙවන ෙමොකක්වත් නිසා ෙනොෙවයි. අෙප් රට නැවතත් ෙබදුම්වාදය ශක්තිමත් කරන දිශාවට රැෙගන ගිහින්, අෙප් රෙට් ෙකොටි තස්තවාදය ශක්තිමත් කරන දිශාවට රැෙගන යෑෙම් ඔවුන්ෙග් කටයුත්ත සිදු කරමින් ඉන්නවා. ඒ වාෙග්ම ෙම් රෙට් මානව හිමිකම් කඩ ෙවනවා; ෙම් රට ඇතුෙළේ දකුෙණ් ෙමන්න ෙම් වාෙග් භීතියක් ඇති ෙවලා තිෙබනවා; දකුෙණ් ජන ජීවිතය ෙමෙහම කඩාකප්පල් ෙවලා තිෙබනවා; අසරණ මිනිසුන් මිය යනවාය කියන කාරණය මතක් කරමින් ෙම් රටට ජාතɕන්තර පජාවෙග් අවධානය දිනා ගැනීම සඳහා, අවධානය ෙයොමු කරවන්න රාජɕ ෙනොවන සංවිධාන මැදිහත් ෙවමින් ඉන්නවා. ඒ නිසා ඉතාමත් පැහැදිලියි, ෙම් තිෙබන පබල වුවමනාව. ෙකොටි හිතවාදී මාධɕය ඒ කටයුත්තට කර උර ෙදමින් ඉන්නවා. සමහර මාධɕ ආයතන ඒ කටයුත්තට කර උර ෙදමින් ඉන්නවා, ඉතාමත් ඍජුව සහ වකව. ඒ නිසා ෙකොටින්ෙග් ෙම් තස්තවාදී වුවමනාවන්, බටහිර වුවමනාවන්, ඒ වාෙග්ම රාජɕ ෙනොවන සංවිධානවල වුවමනාවන් පරාජය කරලා, යුදමය ෙලස ෙකොටි තස්තවාදීන් පරාජය කිරීෙම් කටයුත්ත තුළින් ෙම් රටට ෙගෞරවාන්විත සාමය රැෙගන ඒෙම් කටයුත්ත තමයි පථම, අංක එෙක් කාර්යය ෙවලා තිෙබන්ෙන්.

මූලාසනාරූඪ ගරු මන්තීතුමනි, ඒ වාෙග්ම මා ඉතාමත් වැදගත් කරුණක් ෙම් ෙමොෙහොෙත් කියන්න ඕනෑකම තිෙබනවා. විෙශේෂෙයන් පසු ගිය කාල පරිච්ෙඡ්දෙය් ෙමොණරාගල දිස්තික්කෙය්, ඒ වෙග්ම අම්පාර දිස්තික්කෙය්, - බදුල්ල දිස්තික්කෙය්ත් සමහර තැන්වල - ෙපො ෙලොන්නරුව, අනුරාධපුරය වාෙග් දිස්තික්ක ගණනාවක සිදු වුණු සමහර පහාරයන් හරහා අනාරක්ෂිත ගම්මාන, එල්ටීටීඊ තර්ජන ඇති විය හැකි ගම්මාන ගණනාවක් ඇති ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. අනාරක්ෂිත ගම්මාන පමාණයක් ඇති ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ඒ ගම්මාන සඳහා කමවත් ආරක්ෂිත වැඩ පිළිෙවළක් නිර්මාණය ෙවන්න ඕනෑ. එල්ටීටීඊ තස්තවාදය හමුෙව් බියට පත් වන ජනතාවක් ෙවනුවට, එඩිතරව, හමුදා ෙමෙහයුම් සමඟ යුදමය ෙලස ෙකොටි තස්තවාදය පරාජය කරන කටයුත්ත ශක්තිමත් කර ගැනීමට උර ෙදන ජනතාවක් තුළින් ඒ අනාරක්ෂිත ගම්මාන ආරක්ෂා කරන වැඩ පිළිෙවළක් පථමෙයන් ඇති කර ගත යුතුව තිෙබනවා. අප දන්නවා, පසු ගිය කාලෙය් කැබිතිෙගොල්ලෑව පහාරය සිදු වුණු කාලෙය් රජෙය් අවධානය ෙයොමු ෙවලා, අ ෙප් පැත්ෙතනුත් තිබුණු සමහර ෙයෝජනා සැලකිල්ලට අරෙගන ඒ අනාරක්ෂිත ගම්මාන ආශිත සිවිල් ආරක්ෂක කමිටු පිහිටු වීෙම් කටයුත්ත ආරම්භ කළ බව. නමුත් ඒක පළමු පැෙය්ම ආරම්භ කරලා, දණි පනි ගහලා පටන් ගත්තාට ඒ සිවිල් ආරක්ෂක කමිටු සවිබල ගැන්වීෙම්, සජීවි කර

[ගරු ආර්. එම්. පත්ම උදයශාන්ත ගුණෙසේකර මහතා]

2008 ෙපබරවාරි 06 743 744

ගන්න එෙක්, කියාත්මක කර ගන්න එෙක් අඩු පාඩුකම් පමාණයක් තිබුණා. ඒ නිසා දැන් අතɕවශɕ ෙවලා තිෙබනවා, සිවිල් ආරක්ෂක කමිටු සකිය කර ගැනීෙම් කටයුත්ත. ෙම් දිනවල නැවතත් සිවිල් ආරක්ෂක කමිටු කැඳවා ෙගන යනවා. ඒ ඇතුෙළත් අඩු පාඩුකම් පමාණයක් තිෙබනවා. මූලාසනාරූඪ ගරු මන්තීතුමනි, ෙමොණරාගල දිස්තික්කෙය් ගම්මාන ගණනාවකට මා ෙපෞද්ගලිකව ගියා. ඒ හැම ගම්මානයකටම යද්දී නැගුණු මැසිවිල්ල තමයි, ෙචෝදනාව තමයි, “අපි දන්ෙන් නැහැ, ආරක්ෂක කියා මාර්ග සම්බන්ධව අපි හරියට දැනුවත් ෙවලා නැහැ, අෙප් ගෙම් සිවිල් ආරක්ෂක කමිටුව කැඳවලා නැහැ කියන කාරණය; ගමට ගිනි අවි ලබා දීලා තිෙබනවා තමයි, නමුත් ගත යුතු කියාමාර්ග සම්බන්ධව අපට ෙහොඳ හැටි අවෙබෝධයක් නැහැ” කියන කාරණය. ෙම් වන ෙකොටත් යම් යම් ආරක්ෂක කියාමාර්ග අරෙගන තිෙබනවා තමයි. සිවිල් ආරක්ෂක බලකායක් බඳවා ගැනීමට කටයුතු ආරම්භ ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ගාමාරක්ෂක බලකාය බඳවා ගැනීෙම් කටයුතු දිස්තික්ක ගණනාවකම ආරම්භ ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. සිවිල් ආරක්ෂක කමිටු පිහිටු වීම සම්බන්ධව සහ ඒවා සකිය කර ගැනීෙම් වැඩ ෙකොටස් ආරම්භ ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. හමුදා ෙමෙහයුම් ගණනාවක් තුළින් ඒ පෙද්ශවල ෙසෝදිසි ෙමෙහයුම් සිදු ෙවනවා. ෙපොලිස් මාර්ග බාධක දමලා හදිසි ෙමෙහයුම්, වැටලීම් මඟින් සැක කටයුතු තැන් අනාවරණය කර ගනිමින් අවශɕ ෙමෙහයුම් සිදු කරමින් ඉන්නවා. නමුත්, ෙම් හරහා සිදු විය යුතු අනිවාර්ය කාර්යයක් තමයි, ඒ සියලුම අනාරක්ෂිත ගම්මාන ආරක්ෂා කර ගැනීෙම් වැඩ පිළිෙවළක් ඇති කිරීම. මූලාසනාරූඪ ගරු මන්තීතුමනි, තණමල්විල පෙද්ශෙය් කලවැල්ගල, හම්ෙබ්ගමුව, අරෙඹ්ගම, කහකුරුල්ලන්පැලැස්ස, අඟුණුෙකොළපැලැස්ස වෙග් පෙද්ශවල ගම්මාන අද අනාරක්ෂිත ගම්මාන බවට පත් ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ඒ වාෙග්ම මහවැව, කිතුල්ෙකොෙට්, කුඩාඔය, ෙතලුල්ල, ලුණුගම්ෙවෙහර හා ෙබරලිෙහල වෙග් පෙද්ශවල අනාරක්ෂිත ගම්මාන පමාණයක් ඇති ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. මිනිස්සු භයට පත් ෙවලා තිෙබනවා; භීතියට පත් ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. සවස හය හත වන ෙකොට මිනිස්සු ගෙමන් පිටතට යන තත්ත්වයට පත් ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ඒ නිසාම ඒ ගම්වල මිනිසුන් ජීවත් ෙවන්න බැරි තත්ත්වයට පත් ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ෙහේන් ෙගොවිතැන් අත හැර දමන තත්ත්වයක් ඇති ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. කුඹුරු ෙගොවිතැන් අත හැර දමන තත්ත්වයක් ඇති ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ඒ නිසා ඒ ෙගොවිතැන් ආරක්ෂා කර ගැනීෙම් වැඩ පිළිෙවළක් රජය පැත්ෙතන් අනිවාර්යෙයන් ෙයොදන්න ඕනෑ. ඒ පෙද්ශවල ෙගොවිතැන් අත හැර දැමීම නිසා රුපියල් ෙකෝටි ගණනක් පාඩු ලබා තිෙබනවා. ඒ ෙගොවියන්ෙග් පැත්ෙතනුයි. ෙගොවියන්ෙග් ෙගොවිතැන් ආරක්ෂා කර ෙගන, ෙහේන් ෙගොවියන්ෙග් ෙගොවිතැන් ආරක්ෂා කර ෙගන, ෙමවර කන්නෙය් අස්වැන්න ෙනළා ගැනීම සඳහා අවශɕ ආරක්ෂක කියා මාර්ග ඒ පෙද්ශවල සිදු කරන්න ඕනෑ.

මූලාසනාරූඪ ගරු මන්තීතුමනි, ඒ වාෙග්ම වැල්ලවාය පෙද්ශෙය්ත් අනාරක්ෂිත ගම්මාන පමාණයක් තිෙබනවා. ආනපල්ලම, වැල්ලවාය, පැල්වත්ත පෙද්ශෙය් හා බුත්තල පෙද්ශෙය් බ්ෙලොක් 3, 4, 5, 6, 7, 14, වන්දම හා ෙදමලිය කියන ගම්මාන ෙකොටි තස්තවාදීන්ෙග් බිය ඇති වී තිෙබන පෙද්ශයි; තස්තවාදීන්ෙග් තර්ජන ඇති විය හැකි පෙද්ශයි. ඒ වාෙග්ම බුත්තල ෙහලගම, ෙගෝනගං ආර, ඔක්කම්පිටිය, මාලිගාවිල, නියදැල්ල, මිනිපුරගම, දෙඹ්යාය, නුගමණ්ඩිය හා ගල්ටැම්මණ්ඩිය වෙග් පෙද්ශ ෙම් තුළින් අනාරක්ෂිත ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ෙමොනරාගල පාෙද්ශීය ෙල්කම් ෙකොට්ඨාසෙය් සුදුවතුර ආර, හුලංදාව, හුලංදාව දකුණ හා වම, ෙතනගල්ලන්ද, ෙබෝහිටිය, අම්පිටිය හා ෙකොෙලොංහින්න වෙග් පෙද්ශ අනාරක්ෂිත ගම්මාන බවට පත් ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. සියඹලාණ්ඩුව, ඇතිමෙල්, ෙකොටියාගල, වත්ෙත්ගම, මහකලුෙගොල්ල, උඩකැපූ ආර, 6 කණුව හා 9 කණුව කියන ප ɡෙද්ශවල අනාරක්ෂිත ගම්මාන ගණනාවක් අනාරක්ෂිත ෙවලයි තිෙබන්ෙන්.

ඒ වාෙග්ම මඩුල්ල පාෙද්ශීය ෙල්කම් ෙකොට්ඨාසෙය් ඉඟිණියාගල, බදුලුෙවල, ගල්ගමුව, ෙනල්ලියද්ද හා මුල්ෙල්ගම පෙද්ශ අනාරක්ෂිත ගම්මාන බවට පත් ෙවලා තිෙබනවා; එල්ටීටීඊ

තර්ජන ඇති විය හැකි ගම්මාන බවට පත් ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. නිල්ගල පෙද්ශෙයන්, යාල උතුර හා දකුණ ප ɡෙද්ශෙයන් ෙම් පෙද්ශයට කුඩා කුඩා කණ්ඩායම් වශෙයන් ෙකොටි තස්තවාදීන් ඇතුළු ෙවලා කියලයි සැක කරන්ෙන්. ඒ වාෙග්ම බදුල්ල දිස්තික්කෙය් මහියංගනය පාෙද්ශීය ෙල්කම් ෙකොට්ඨාසෙය් ඇකිරියන්කුඹුර, අරලුපිටිය, ෙදහිගම, ෙසේරුපිටිය, ෙමොරාන, තලාෙව්ගම, කුකුලාෙපොල හා දඹාන යන පෙද්ශවල එවැනි අනාරක්ෂිත ගම්මාන ඇති ෙවලා තිෙබනවා.

මූලාසනාරූඪ ගරු මන්තීතුමනි, වැල්ලවාය පාෙද්ශීය ෙල්කම් ෙකොට්ඨාසෙය් හා ෙමොනරාගල පාෙද්ශීය ෙල්කම් ෙකොට්ඨාසෙය් සමහර ගම්මානවලට ගිනි අවි ලබා දීෙම්දී ඉතාමත් අවිධිමත් වැඩ පිළිෙවළක් ආරම්භ ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ෙද්ශපාලනඥයන්ෙග් හිතවත් අයෙග් නාම ෙල්ඛනවලට ගිනි අවි ලබා දීෙම් කටයුත්තක් සිද්ධ ෙවලා තිබුණා. අප ෙම් පිළිබඳව මාධɕවලට කිව්වා. ආරක්ෂක ෙල්කම්තුමාට කිව්වා, වහාම ෙම්ක විධිමත් කරන්න, එෙහම නැත්නම් නීතිවිෙරෝධී පිරිස්වලට ගිනි අවි ලැබීම තුළින් ෙවනත් ෙද්ශපාලන පශ්න ඇති ෙවන්න පුළුවන්කම තිෙබනවාය කියලා. ෙද්ශපාලනඥයන්ෙග් හිතවතුන් තමයි, සමහර නාම ෙල්ඛන හදලා තිබුෙණ්. ෙමොනරාගල පාෙද්ශීය ෙල්කම් ෙකොට්ඨාසෙය් එක්තරා ගමක තත්ත්වය ගැන බලන්න. පාෙද්ශීය සභා මන්තීවරෙයක් ගිනි අවියක් අරෙගන, එක්තරා ගම්මානයක කන්දක් උඩට ගිහින්, ෙකොටි එනවාය කියලා ෙවඩි තැබීම නිසා ගම්මාන පිටින්ම ඒ පෙද්ශ අත හැරලා ගියා. ඒ නිසා ෙම්ක ඉතා වග කීෙමන් කරන්න ඕනෑ. ආරක්ෂක ෙල්කම්තුමාට අප ෙම් කාරණය අවධාරණය කරනවා. ආරක්ෂක කියා මාර්ග ගැනීම සම්බන්ධව ආරක්ෂක ඇමතිවරයාට අප කියනවා, විධිමත් පරිදි සිවිල් ආරක්ෂක කමිටු පිහිටුවා, ඒ ගිනි අවි ලබා දීෙම් සහ ඒ පෙද්ශ ආරක්ෂා කර ගැනීෙම් වැඩ පිළිෙවෙළේදී විධිමත් ෙලස කටයුතු කරන්නය කියලා.

ඒ වාෙග්ම ඒ පෙද්ශවල ජනතාවෙග් ෛධර්යය, ශක්තිය වැඩි කර ගැනීම සඳහා ඒ ගම්මාන මට්ටමින් කිසි යම් කම ෙව්දයක් අවශɕ ෙවනවා. ඒ වාෙග්ම ගාමාරක්ෂක බලකාය පමාණවත් පරිදි බඳවා ගැනීෙම් කටයුත්තක් ආරම්භ කරන්න ඕනෑ. ගාමාරක්ෂක බලකාය පමාණවත් පරිදි බඳවා ගන්නවා වෙග්ම සිවිල් ආරක්ෂක ෙසේවය ශක්තිමත් කර ගැනීෙම්දී ඒ පෙද්ශ දැනුවත් කිරීෙම් කටයුත්තක් සිදු ෙවන්න ඕනෑ.

මූලාසනාරූඪ මන්තීතුමා (தைலைமதாங்கும் உᾠப்பினர் அவர்கள்) (The Presiding Member) ගරු මන්තීතුමනි, ඔබතුමාෙග් කථාව දැන් අවසන් කරන්න.

ගරු ආර්. එම්. පත්ම උදයශාන්ත ගුණෙසේකර මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ஆர். எம். பத்ம உதயஷாந்த குணேசகர) (The Hon. R. M. Padma Udayashantha Gunasekera) මා අවසන් කරනවා, මූලාසනාරූඪ ගරු මන්තීතුමනි. ඒ තස්තවාදය හමුෙව් බියට පත් ෙවලා තිෙබන පෙද්ශවල ආරක්ෂාව සඳහා ෙම් කටයුතු සිදු කරනවා වෙග්ම, ඒ පෙද්ශවල පූර්ණ ෙලස ෙසෝදිසි ෙමෙහයුම් සඳහා අවශɕ ආරක්ෂක කියා මාර්ග ගැනීම තුළින් ආරක්ෂක හමුදාව සහ ෙපොලීසිය ලබා තිෙබන සමහර දුෂ්කරතා පියමං කරන්න ඒ ආරක්ෂක හමුදාව සහ ෙපොලීසිය ෙවත සම්පූර්ණ සහෙයෝගය ලබා දීමට අවශɕ කටයුතු ලෑස්ති කරන්නය කියන කාරණය රජය පැත්තට ෙයොමු කරමින් මා නවතිනවා. ෙබොෙහොම ස්තුතියි.

මූලාසනාරූඪ මන්තීතුමා (தைலைமதாங்கும் உᾠப்பினர் அவர்கள்) (The Presiding Member) ඊ ළඟට ගරු (පූජɕ) එල්ලාවල ෙම්ධානන්ද ස්වාමීන් වහන්ෙසේ. ඔබ වහන්ෙසේට විනාඩි 18ක් තිෙබනවා.

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 745 746

[අ.භා. 12.51]

ගරු (පූජɕ) එල්ලාවල ෙම්ධානන්ද හිමි (மாண்ᾗமிகு (வண.) எல்லாவல ேமதானந்த ேதரர்) (The Hon. (Ven.) Ellawala Medhananda Thero) විනාඩි 20ක් තිබුණා, මූලාසනාරූඪ ගරු මන්තීතුමනි. මූලාසනාරූඪ ගරු මන්තීතුමනි, හදිසි නීතිය තවත් මසකින් දී ර්ඝ කිරීෙම් ෙයෝජනාව විවාද කරන අද දිනෙය්දී මා කරුණු දක්වන්ෙන්, ජාතික ෙහළ උරුමය හැටියටයි. මට දැන ගන්න ලැබුණු හැටියට මට විනාඩි 20ක කාලයක් තිබුණා. ඔබතුමා ඒ විනාඩි 20 මට ලබා ෙදයි කියලා මා බලාෙපොෙරොත්තු ෙවනවා. අද ෙම් රෙට් තස්තවාදයක් තිෙබන බව කැමැත්ෙතන් ෙහෝ අකැමැත්ෙතන් ෙහෝ අප ෙකොයි කාටත් පිළිගන්න සිදු ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ජාති පශ්නයක් නැතිව, ආගම් පශ්නයක් නැතිව අවුරුදු 25කට වැඩි කාලයක් මුළුල්ෙල් ෙම් රෙට් ජන ජීවිතයට ෙම් තස්තවාදය තදින් බල පා තිෙබනවා. පසු ගිය කාල වකවානුව තුළ ෙම් තස්තවාදය තීරණාත්මකව අවසන් කිරීමට අවස්ථා උදා ෙවලා තිබුණත්, තිවිධ හමුදාවට, ෙපොලීසියට, ෙපොලිස් විෙශේෂ කාර්ය බලකායට සහ සිවිල් ෙසේවා බලකායට ඒ සඳහා නියම ෙද්ශපාලන නායකත්වයක් තිබුෙණ් නැති බව අපට ෙපෙනනවා. කකුෙලන් අදින නායකත්වය නිසා තිවිධ හමුදාෙව් ෙම් වන විට සිටිය යුතු වැදගත් නිලධාරින්, රණ විරුවන් විශාල සංඛɕාවක් අපට අහිමි වුණා. ඒ වෙග්ම මැති ඇමැතිවරුන් අහිමි වුණා; ආරක්ෂක ඇමතිවරුන් අහිමි වුණා; ජනාධිපතිවරු අහිමි වුණා. ෙම් තත්ත්වය ඇති වුෙණ් තස්තවාදය තීරණාත්මකව අවසන් කිරීෙම් සංකල්පයක් නැත්නම් අදහසක් ෙද්ශපාලන නායකත්වය තුළ ෙනොතිබීම නිසායි. අද ඒ පශ්නය විසඳිලා තිෙබනවා. ෙම් රෙට් ජනතාව ෙකොෙහොමද සාමකාමීව ජීවත් ෙවන්න ඕනෑ, ෙකොෙහොමද ෙම් රට සංවර්ධනය කරන්න ඕනෑ, ෙකොෙහොමද ෙම් රෙට් සංස්කෘතිය දියුණු කරන්න ඕනෑ, මහජනතාවෙග් අවශɕතා ෙමොනවාද කියන එක ගැන පැහැදිලි අවෙබෝධයක් තිෙබන ෙද්ශපාලන නායකත්වයක්, රට ගැන හිතන නායකත්වයක් අද ඇති ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ඒ නායකත්වය තුළින් තිවිධ හමුදාවට, ෙපොලීසියට, විෙශේෂ කාර්ය බලකායට සහ සිවිල් ෙසේවා බලකායට ෙකොන්ද ෙකළින් තියා ෙගන තමන්ෙග් රාජකාරිය කරන්න පුළුවන් ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ඒ නිසා අද රෙට් ජනතාව තුළ තිවිධ හමුදාව ෙක ෙරහිත්, ආරක්ෂක අංශ ෙකෙරහිත්, රාජɕ නායකත්වය ෙකෙරහිත් දැඩි විශ්වාසයක් ෙගොඩ නැඟී තිෙබනවා, වැඩි කල් යන්න ෙපරාතුව ෙම් රෙට් සාමකාමීව ජීවත් ෙවන්න පුළුවන් වාතාවරණයක් ඇති ෙවයි කියා. ඔවුන් තුළ ඒ අෙප්ක්ෂාව තිෙබනවා. ඒ අෙප්ක්ෂාව මුදුන් පත් කර වීම සඳහා දැඩි කැප වීමකින් සියලු ෙදනාම කියාත්මක ෙවනවා. ජනතාවක් වශෙයන්, ෙද්ශපාලන පක්ෂ වශෙයන් ෙමතැනදී අෙපනුත් කිසියම් කැප වීමක් අවශɕයි. ජනතාවට සාමය උදා කිරීම
